# Changelog

## [3.0.0](https://www.github.com/christopherthielen/deck/compare/v2.1064.0...v3.0.0) (2021-03-01)


### âš  BREAKING CHANGES

* **plugins:** Switch plugin-manifest to json to match the json output from gate's /plugins/deck/plugin-manifest.json
* **plugins:** Switch plugin-manifest to json to match the json output from gate's /plugins/deck/plugin-manifest.json
* **plugins:** * feat(plugins): Load plugins and plugin manifest from gate Load from gate URL: /plugins/deck/plugin-manifest.json Continues to load pre-baked manifest information from the local deck asset /plugin-manifest.js
* **travis:** This will add a new Travis trigger and a new Travis stage. Corresponds with https://github.com/spinnaker/echo/pull/141 and https://github.com/spinnaker/orca/pull/1213.
